<p class="heading"><span class="col_xi" refersTo="page_0011"/>ACTS OF THE SESSION.</p>

<p>II.&#x2014;In Chronological Order.</p>

<p>40&#x2014;&#x2019;27.&#x2014;<noteRef href="note02_p11" marker="&#x2020;"/>Union Nationality and Flags.</p>

<p>41&#x2014;&#x2019;27.&#x2014;<noteRef href="note02_p11" marker="&#x2020;"/>Orange Free State Marriage Law Amendment.</p>

<p>42&#x2014;&#x2019;27.&#x2014;<noteRef href="note02_p11" marker="&#x2020;"/>Psorosis.</p>

<p>43&#x2014;&#x2019;27.&#x2014;<noteRef href="note01_p11" marker="*"/>Marburg Immigration Settlement (Local Board of Management).</p>

<p>44&#x2014;&#x2019;27.&#x2014;<noteRef href="note01_p11" marker="*"/>Precious Stones.</p>

<p>1&#x2014;&#x2019;28.&#x2014;<noteRef href="note01_p11" marker="*"/>Diamond Trade Regulation (Natal).</p>

<p>2&#x2014;&#x2019;28.&#x2014;<noteRef href="note02_p11" marker="&#x2020;"/>Additional Appropriation (1927-&#x2019;28).</p>

<p>3&#x2014;&#x2019;28.&#x2014;<noteRef href="note02_p11" marker="&#x2020;"/>Appropriation (Part).</p>

<p>4&#x2014;&#x2019;28.&#x2014;<noteRef href="note02_p11" marker="&#x2020;"/>Railways and Harbours Additional Appropriation (1927-&#x2019;28).</p>

<p class="heading"><span class="col_I1" refersTo="page_0013"/>INDEX TO SUBJECTS.</p>

<p>In this index &#x201C;R&#x201D; denotes &#x201C;Reading.&#x201D;</p>

<p>The sign &#x2020; indicates that the Bill or other matter concerned dropped owing to the prorogation of Parliament.</p>

<p>Matters which have been given headings in this index may also form the subject of questions and will be found separately indexed under the headings &#x201C;Questions&#x201D; or &#x201C;Oral Questions.&#x201D;</p>

<p><b>SPEAKER AND DEPUTY-SPEAKER (Rulings and Observations by)&#x2014;</b></p>

<ul>

<li>Acts of Parliament&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Reflections may not be made on, 66.</li>

<li>When Act with Dutch text is amended, the phraseology of the amending Bill must be in Afrikaans, but words or sections to be incorporated in such Act must be in Dutch, 2283.</li></ul></li>

<li>Additional Estimates&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Details should be discussed in Committee, 1516.</li>

<li>Discussion confined to matters in, 1734, 1736.</li>

<li>Policy, matters of general, not open to discussion on motion to go into Committee on, 1513.</li></ul></li>

<li>Adjournment, motion for&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Of debate&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>May not be twice moved by same member in same debate, 2361.</li>

<li>May not include proposal as to date of resumption, 642.</li>

<li>Member moving, does not lose right to speak on main question, 2361.</li></ul></li></ul></li>

<li>On definite matter of urgent public importance&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>May not be moved&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>If matter not of such urgency that it cannot be met by giving notice, 594.</li>

<li>If subject has been previously dealt with by way of official statements from time to time, 4848.</li></ul></li>

<li>Preliminary statement must be brief, 443, 594.</li></ul></li>

<li>Amendments&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>May not be moved&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>In Select Committee reversing principle of Bill, 1627.</li>

<li>Involving expenditure. 1422, 4829, 4830.</li>

<li>To motion or amendment by member who has moved or seconded such motion or amendment, 223, 2367, 3693.</li></ul></li>

<li>Must be relevant, 214-5.</li>

<li>To Bills (<i>see</i> &#x201C;Bills&#x201D;).</li>

<li>To message to Senate, may be moved, 418.</li></ul></li>

<li>Anticipation (<i>see</i> &#x201C;Debate&#x201D;).</li>

<li>Appeal from ruling of Chairman of Committees&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>As to non-competency of two clauses being before Committee on a Bill at the same time (2566-7), 2568.</li></ul></li>

<li>Auditor-General, reflections on or charges against, may not be made unless based on substantive motion, 4850 (<i>see</i> also &#x201C;Auditor-General&#x201D; under &#x201C;Chairman&#x201D; and 4851).</li>

<li>Bills&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Amendments&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Appeal from Chairman&#x2019;s ruling as to non-competency of two clauses being before Committee at same time (2566-7), 2568.</li>

<li>May be moved to motion for leave to introduce, 2793.</li>

<li>May not be moved&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Introducing new principles, after second reading. 1700, 2791-4.</li>

<li>Outside scope and irrelevant to subject of Bill, 4970.</li>

<li>Reversing principle, after second reading, 1627.</li>

<li>To clauses on third reading, 2486.</li></ul></li>

<li>On report stage&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Method of reversing decision taken in Committee, 3410.</li>

<li>Notice of, required, 3502, 3715; but if owing to circumstances notice could not be given Speaker may allow, if in order, 4970.</li></ul></li></ul></li>

<li>Outside scope of Bill but sufficiently relevant to its provisions, require an instruction, 1168.</li>

<li>Instruction to Committee of Whole House on&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Notice of, will be accepted in certain circumstances after proper time for giving, 2865.</li>

<li><span class="col_I47" refersTo="page_0059"/>To cure irregularity of Select Committee of inserting clause not within scope of Bill referred to it but sufficiently relevant to provisions of measure, required, 1168.</li></ul></li>

<li>Introduction of&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Amendment may be moved to motion for, 2793.</li>

<li>Provisions may not be incorporated not covered by motion for leave to introduce (clause expunged), 1383.</li>

<li>Special leave required to move for leave to introduce if notice has not been given, 2789.</li></ul></li>

<li>Language of&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>When Act with Dutch text is amended, phraseology of amending Bill must be in Afrikaans but any words or sections to be incorporated in such Act must be in Dutch, 2283.</li></ul></li>

<li>Provisions may not be incorporated not covered by title or by order for leave to introduce (clause expunged), 1383.</li>

<li>Re-committal of, discussion confined to question of, 2203, 2213.</li>

<li>Report stage of&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Amendments on (<i>see</i> &#x201C;Amendments&#x2019;&#x201D; above).</li>

<li>Clause may be allowed to stand over, 3463.</li></ul></li>

<li>Revival of&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Bill may be revived notwithstanding fact that it is identical with measure before House during session antecedent to that preceding session in which leave to revive is sought, 1238.</li></ul></li>

<li>Third reading of&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Amendments may not be moved to clauses on, 2486.</li></ul></li>

<li>Two stages of, may not be taken at same sitting if objection taken, 1683.</li></ul></li>

<li>Committee of Whole House&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Speaker cannot deal with matters that occurred in, not referred to him, 4851.</li></ul></li>

<li>Debate&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Anticipation not in order&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Of matter on Order Paper, 1752.</li></ul></li>

<li>Closes when member in charge of motion has replied, 2398, 4830.</li>

<li>Discussion irregular&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Upon matters sub judice, 3459.</li>

<li>Upon notice of motion, 288.</li>

<li>Upon proceedings in Select Committee not yet reported to House, 774, 3109, 3955, 3970.</li>

<li>Upon proceedings in Senate, 408.</li>

<li>When no question before House, 2811, 3405, 3568, 4965.</li></ul></li>

<li>Interruption not in order, 442, 2150, 3138, 4840.</li>

<li>Language of speech may not be changed (save in case of member in charge of business before House), 541.</li>

<li>Members&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Reflections or accusations may not be made on or against (<i>see</i> &#x201C;Unparliamentary language&#x201D; below).</li>

<li>Word of, must be accepted, 365, 378.</li>

<li><i>See</i> also &#x201C;Order in debate&#x201D; below.</li></ul></li>

<li>Not closed by moving of &#x201C;previous question&#x201D;, 463.</li>

<li>Not points of order&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Order in&#x2014;

<ul>

<li>Member must address the Chair, 453.</li>

<li>Private member may not speak from Ministerial benches, 1637.</li></ul></li>

<li>Personal charges (<i>see</i> &#x201C;Auditor-General&#x201D;).</li>

<ul>

<li>Allowed after question asked and replied to, 1231.</li>

<li>Repetition (tedious) not permitted, 4997.</li>

<li>Must be relevant to original question, 1230, 1384, 1472, 1639, 2318, 2326, 2331, 2595, 3523, 3848-9, 4425, 4840, 5007; otherwise notice should be given, 1126, 2013-4, 2020-2.</li>
